## Live GitHub Issue Records

### Issue #56: folio convert rejects .docx files — normalization gate too narrow

- URL: https://github.com/ohjonathan/folio.love/issues/56

- State at triage: OPEN

- Created: 2026-04-16T16:30:52Z

- Updated: 2026-05-12T19:23:15Z

- Labels: none

#### Body

## Summary

`folio convert` rejects `.docx` files with `Unsupported format: .docx` at the normalization stage, even though `markitdown` (used internally for text extraction) supports DOCX natively.

## Reproduction

```bash
folio convert "./path/to/sow.docx" --client Acme --engagement "Build"
```

```
Converting: sow.docx
  Normalizing to PDF...
✗ Conversion failed: Unsupported format: .docx
```

## Context

Real consulting corpora frequently contain `.docx` artifacts (SOWs, contracts, terms sheets, design documents). Today the workaround is to manually export to PDF via Word, then convert the PDF. This adds an operator step that breaks automation and `folio batch` workflows.

## Suggested behavior

Accept `.docx` at the normalization gate. Since DOCX is not slide-oriented:
- Skip slide image extraction (or render page images via a document renderer)
- Use `markitdown` for full-document text extraction (already works)
- Produce a single evidence note with the full document body rather than per-slide sections

Alternatively, expose a `folio convert --format document` flag that opts into a document-oriented pipeline rather than the slide-oriented one.

## Environment

- folio-love 0.6.4
- macOS 25.4.0
- Python 3.12


### Issue #61: folio ingest: native .eml / email thread support

- URL: https://github.com/ohjonathan/folio.love/issues/61

- State at triage: OPEN

- Created: 2026-04-17T04:29:35Z

- Updated: 2026-05-12T19:23:17Z

- Labels: none

#### Body

## Summary

`folio` does not natively handle `.eml` files. Email threads — a critical class of consulting engagement evidence — currently require a custom parsing step (extract headers, reconstruct quoted thread, strip Outlook noise, render markdown) before they can be fed into `folio ingest --type internal_sync`. A first-class email pipeline would close a significant gap in the format coverage story alongside #56.

## Today's workaround

On a live engagement we wrote a ~370-line `scripts/parse_emails.py` to:
- Parse `.eml` via Python's `email` stdlib
- Extract envelope headers (From, To, CC, Date, Subject)
- Reconstruct the quoted thread by splitting on Outlook's `From: ...` / `Date: ...` blocks
- Sort messages chronologically (oldest-first), with the outermost message dated from the EML envelope
- Strip noise: `<tel:>` / `<mailto:>` / `<https://disclaimer-link>` wrappers, Zoom dial-in tables, SIP/H.323 lines, `____________` separators, repeated signatures, external-sender warnings, scotiabank/firm-wide disclaimers
- Collapse Outlook's split bullets (`*` on one line, content on the next) into proper markdown bullets
- Catalog attachments by filename + MIME type (no binary extraction)

The resulting markdown then ingests cleanly via:

```bash
folio ingest <thread.md> \
  --type internal_sync \
  --date <YYYY-MM-DD> \
  --client <Client> \
  --engagement <Engagement> \
  --participants \"<comma-separated-names>\"
```

For a 3-thread, 11-attachment Scotiabank corpus this produced 3 `review_status: clean` interaction notes with 28 total claims extracted via the Anthropic fallback (Sonnet 4 took over after the OpenAI route 403'd at the AI Gateway).

## Suggested behavior

### 1. New document type: `correspondence`

Email threads aren't really meetings. Add a sibling to `interaction` and `evidence`:

```yaml
type: correspondence
subtype: email_thread  # or email_single
```

This avoids overloading `internal_sync` and gives consumers (e.g., the Folio Library cursor rule) a cleaner lookup vocabulary.

### 2. New CLI: `folio ingest-email <path.eml>`

Or extend `folio ingest` with `--type email_thread` and accept `.eml` directly. Required behavior:

- Parse all `text/plain` parts; fall back to `html` -> markdown via `markitdown`
- Reconstruct the thread (oldest-first); preserve per-message From/To/CC/Date in frontmatter
- Strip Outlook/Zoom/disclaimer noise (a curated rules list will get most of it)
- Resolve participants from To/CC/From across the thread (deduplicated, normalized)
- Catalog attachments in frontmatter:
  ```yaml
  attachments:
    - filename: SOW_v9.docx
      content_type: application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.wordprocessingml.document
      size_bytes: 2140160
      sha256: <hash>
  ```
- Optionally extract attachment bodies into the registry (gated by `--extract-attachments`) so that PDFs and images on the thread become first-class documents and can be `impacts:`-linked back to the email

### 3. Registry / frontmatter additions

```yaml
sender: Mishal Desai <Mishal_Desai@mckinsey.com>
recipients_to: [Jake Itzkowitz, Tim Vogeler, ...]
recipients_cc: [Pankaj Kumar, ...]
thread_message_count: 11
attachment_count: 3
external_thread: false   # true if any party is non-McKinsey
```

### 4. Enrichment hints

The `enrich` step would benefit from email-aware heuristics:
- Quoted blocks (markdown `>`) should be lower-weight than primary author content
- Signatures should be detected and excluded from claim extraction
- Decisions that show up in the most recent message should be boosted

## Why this matters

For a typical engagement, the email thread is where decisions are actually made and where vendor positions are first surfaced. The Scotia corpus we just ingested includes a Microsoft solutions-engineer pitch on Azure vs GCP that doesn't appear in any deck or meeting note, but is essential context for the architecture decision. Without first-class email support, this evidence either gets dropped or gets shoehorned into `internal_sync` with awkward titles like \"Re: [External] AI Platform Vendor Decision Points\".

## Related

- #56 (DOCX normalization gate) — same theme: format coverage gaps push real consulting evidence outside Folio's pipeline.

## Environment

- folio-love 0.6.4
- macOS 25.4.0
- Python 3.12
- QuantumBlack AI Gateway (enterprise proxy)


### Issue #62: folio watch <dir>: folder-based auto-ingestion (drop-zone UX)

- URL: https://github.com/ohjonathan/folio.love/issues/62

- State at triage: OPEN

- Created: 2026-04-17T05:03:55Z

- Updated: 2026-05-12T19:23:19Z

- Labels: none

#### Body

## Summary

Add `folio watch <dir>` — a long-running daemon (or `--once` mode for cron / launchd) that monitors a directory for new files and routes each to the appropriate Folio pipeline based on file extension. Closes the "manual CLI invocation per file" gap that today makes Folio feel like a tool you reach for rather than a system that just runs.

## User pain (current state)

To save an email, transcript, deck, or PDF into Folio today, every artifact has the same 4-7 ceremony steps:

1. Get the file into the right subdirectory (`library/<client>/<engagement>/<doctype>/`)
2. Open terminal, `cd` to workspace, `source .env`
3. Remember which Folio verb (`ingest` vs `convert`)
4. Type the right flags (`--type`, `--client`, `--engagement`, `--date`, `--participants`, `--target`)
5. Wait for processing
6. Verify the registry entry was written

Steps 2-6 are 100% mechanical given the file. The user always has the same intent ("this is engagement evidence, file it") but has to translate that into Folio's verb-and-flag vocabulary every single time.

For a solo consultant on a live engagement, this friction is the dominant reason artifacts *don't* end up in Folio — the ceremony cost beats the marginal value of any single file.

## Concrete example from a live engagement

Today, ingesting one email thread on the Scotiabank AI Platform engagement looks like this (from our actual workflow):

```bash
folio ingest \"library/scotiabank/aiplatform/correspondence/2026-04-17_scotia_ai_platform_azure_gcp.md\" \\
  --type internal_sync \\
  --date 2026-04-16 \\
  --client Scotiabank \\
  --engagement \"AI Platform\" \\
  --participants \"Chi Wai Cheung, Jonathan Oh, Bishal Dasgupta, Will Lau\" \\
  --target library/scotiabank/aiplatform/correspondence/ \\
  -n \"Initial ingest from email thread (Azure/GCP agentic stack discussion)\"
```

Seven flags. Six of them have the same value across every email on this engagement, or could be derived from the email's headers. Only `-n` is genuinely per-invocation.

Multiply by a dozen artifacts a day and the reason Folio adoption stalls becomes obvious.

## Proposed feature

    41	def _sample_interaction_registry_entry(**overrides) -> dict:
    42	    defaults = {
    43	        "id": "test_interaction_20260310_call",
    44	        "title": "Test Call",
    45	        "markdown_path": "TestClient/interactions/call/call.md",
    46	        "deck_dir": "TestClient/interactions/call",
    47	        "source_relative_path": "../../../sources/call.txt",
    48	        "source_hash": "abc123def456",
    49	        "source_type": None,
    50	        "version": 1,
    51	        "converted": "2026-03-10T02:15:00Z",
    52	        "modified": "2026-03-10T02:15:00Z",
    53	        "client": "TestClient",
    54	        "authority": "captured",
    55	        "curation_level": "L0",
    56	        "staleness_status": "current",
    57	        "type": "interaction",
    58	        "subtype": "expert_interview",
    59	    }
    60	    defaults.update(overrides)
    61	    return defaults

    63	
    64	def _analysis_result(
    65	    *,
    66	    llm_status: str = "executed",
    67	    review_status: str = "clean",
    68	    tags: list[str] | None = None,
    69	    entities: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,
    70	    provider_name: str | None = "anthropic",
    71	    model_name: str | None = "claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
    72	    fallback_used: bool = False,
    73	) -> InteractionAnalysisResult:
    74	    return InteractionAnalysisResult(
    75	        summary="The team described a successful operational change and a follow-up dependency.",
    76	        tags=tags or ["expert-interview", "operations"],
    77	        entities=entities or {
    78	            "people": ["Jane Smith", "Johnny Oh"],
    79	            "departments": ["Engineering"],
    80	            "systems": ["ServiceNow"],
    81	            "processes": ["Incident Triage"],
    82	        },
    83	        claims=[
    84	            InteractionFinding(
    85	                statement="The team reduced downtime materially.",
    86	                quote="We reduced downtime from 12 hours to 2 hours in one quarter.",
    87	                element_type="data_point",
    88	                confidence="high",
    89	                speaker="Jane Smith",
    90	                validated=True,
    91	            )
    92	        ],
    93	        data_points=[],
    94	        decisions=[
    95	            InteractionFinding(
    96	                statement="The team agreed to add a reporting checkpoint.",
    97	                quote="Add a reporting checkpoint.",
    98	                element_type="decision",
    99	                confidence="medium",
   100	                speaker="Johnny Oh",
   101	                validated=True,
   102	            )
   103	        ],
   104	        open_questions=[],
   105	        notable_quotes=[
   106	            InteractionQuote(
   107	                quote="We reduced downtime from 12 hours to 2 hours in one quarter.",
   108	                element_type="statement",
   109	                confidence="high",
   110	                speaker="Jane Smith",
   111	                validated=True,
   112	            )
   113	        ],
   114	        warnings=[],
   115	        review_status=review_status,
   116	        review_flags=[] if review_status == "clean" else ["analysis_unavailable"],
   117	        extraction_confidence=0.87 if llm_status == "executed" else None,
   118	        grounding_summary={
   119	            "total_claims": 2,
   120	            "high_confidence": 1,
   121	            "medium_confidence": 1,
   122	            "low_confidence": 0,
   123	            "validated": 2,
   124	            "unvalidated": 0,
   125	        },
   126	        pass_strategy="single_pass",
   127	        llm_status=llm_status,
   128	        provider_name=provider_name,
   129	        model_name=model_name,
   130	        fallback_used=fallback_used,
   131	    )
   132	
   133	
   134	def _parse_frontmatter(md_path: Path) -> dict:
   135	    content = md_path.read_text()
   136	    yaml_block = content.split("---", 2)[1].strip()
   137	    return yaml.safe_load(yaml_block)

   140	def _import_org_chart(library: Path) -> Path:
   141	    entities_path = library / "entities.json"
   142	    reg = EntityRegistry(entities_path)
   143	    reg.load()
   144	    import_csv(reg, ROOT_FIXTURE_DIR / "test_org_chart.csv")
   145	    return entities_path

   273	        mock_analyze.return_value = _analysis_result()
   274	
   275	        result = ingest_source(
   276	            config,
   277	            source_path=source,
   278	            subtype="internal_sync",
   279	            event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   280	            client="ClientA",
   281	            engagement="DD Q1 2026",
   282	        )
   283	
   284	        analyzed_text = mock_analyze.call_args.args[0]
   285	        assert "-->" not in analyzed_text
   286	        assert "[00:00:01.200 - 00:00:04.000] Jane Smith: We reduced downtime from 12 hours to 2 hours." in analyzed_text
   287	        assert "[00:00:05.000 - 00:00:07.500] Johnny Oh: Add a reporting checkpoint." in analyzed_text
   288	
   289	        from folio.tracking.sources import compute_file_hash
   290	
   291	        fm = _parse_frontmatter(result.output_path)
   292	        assert fm["source_transcript"].endswith("meeting_export.srt")
   293	        assert fm["source_hash"] == compute_file_hash(source)
   294	
   295	        body = result.output_path.read_text()
   296	        raw_transcript = body.split("> [!quote]- Raw Transcript", 1)[1]
   297	        assert "> [00:00:08.000 - 00:00:10.250] ServiceNow remained the operational backbone." in raw_transcript
   298	
   299	        registry = json.loads((library / "registry.json").read_text())
   300	        entry = registry["decks"][result.interaction_id]
   301	        assert entry["source_relative_path"].endswith("meeting_export.srt")
   302	        assert "source_type" not in entry

   414	    @patch("folio.ingest.analyze_interaction_text")
   415	    def test_reingest_ignores_conflicting_metadata_overrides(self, mock_analyze, tmp_path, caplog):
   416	        library = _make_library(tmp_path)
   417	        source = tmp_path / "transcripts" / "expert_interview.md"
   418	        source.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   419	        shutil.copy2(_fixture("expert_interview.md"), source)
   420	
   421	        config = FolioConfig(library_root=library)
   422	        mock_analyze.side_effect = [_analysis_result(), _analysis_result()]
   423	
   424	        first = ingest_source(
   425	            config,
   426	            source_path=source,
   427	            subtype="expert_interview",
   428	            event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   429	            client="ClientA",
   430	            engagement="DD Q1 2026",
   431	            participants=["Alice", "Bob"],
   432	        )
   433	
   434	        with caplog.at_level("WARNING", logger="folio.ingest"):
   435	            second = ingest_source(
   436	                config,
   437	                source_path=source,
   438	                subtype="expert_interview",
   439	                event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   440	                client="ClientB",
   441	                engagement="DD Q2 2026",
   442	                participants=["Carol"],
   443	            )
   444	
   445	        assert second.version == 2
   446	        fm = _parse_frontmatter(second.output_path)
   447	        assert fm["client"] == "ClientA"
   448	        assert fm["engagement"] == "DD Q1 2026"
   449	        assert fm["participants"] == ["Alice", "Bob"]
   450	
   451	        registry = json.loads((library / "registry.json").read_text())
   452	        entry = registry["decks"][first.interaction_id]
   453	        assert entry["client"] == "ClientA"
   454	        assert entry["engagement"] == "DD Q1 2026"
   455	        assert "Ignoring re-ingest client override" in caplog.text
   456	        assert "Ignoring re-ingest engagement override" in caplog.text
   457	        assert "Ignoring re-ingest participants override" in caplog.text

   496	    @patch("folio.ingest.analyze_interaction_text")
   497	    def test_reingest_preserves_promoted_fields(self, mock_analyze, tmp_path):
   498	        library = _make_library(tmp_path)
   499	        source = tmp_path / "transcripts" / "expert_interview.md"
   500	        source.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   501	        shutil.copy2(_fixture("expert_interview.md"), source)
   502	
   503	        config = FolioConfig(library_root=library)
   504	        first_analysis = _analysis_result()
   505	        second_analysis = _analysis_result()
   506	        second_analysis.summary = "Updated re-ingest summary."
   507	        mock_analyze.side_effect = [first_analysis, second_analysis]
   508	
   509	        first = ingest_source(
   510	            config,
   511	            source_path=source,
   512	            subtype="expert_interview",
   513	            event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   514	            client="ClientA",
   515	            engagement="DD Q1 2026",
   516	        )
   517	
   518	        edited_markdown = (
   519	            first.output_path.read_text()
   520	            .replace("authority: captured\n", "authority: reviewed\n", 1)
   521	            .replace("curation_level: L0\n", "curation_level: L2\n", 1)
   522	        )
   523	        first.output_path.write_text(edited_markdown)
   524	
   525	        second = ingest_source(
   526	            config,
   527	            source_path=source,
   528	            subtype="expert_interview",
   529	            event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   530	            client="ClientA",
   531	            engagement="DD Q1 2026",
   532	        )
   533	
   534	        assert second.version == 2
   535	        fm = _parse_frontmatter(second.output_path)
   536	        assert fm["authority"] == "reviewed"
   537	        assert fm["curation_level"] == "L2"
   538	
   539	        registry = json.loads((library / "registry.json").read_text())
   540	        entry = registry["decks"][second.interaction_id]
   541	        assert entry["authority"] == "reviewed"
   542	        assert entry["curation_level"] == "L2"

   544	    @patch("folio.ingest.analyze_interaction_text")
   545	    def test_reingest_overwrites_analysis(self, mock_analyze, tmp_path):
   546	        library = _make_library(tmp_path)
   547	        source = tmp_path / "transcripts" / "expert_interview.md"
   548	        source.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   549	        shutil.copy2(_fixture("expert_interview.md"), source)
   550	
   551	        config = FolioConfig(library_root=library)
   552	        first_analysis = _analysis_result(review_status="clean")
   553	        first_analysis.summary = "First pass summary."
   554	        first_analysis.review_flags = []
   555	        first_analysis.extraction_confidence = 0.91
   556	
   557	        second_analysis = _analysis_result(review_status="flagged")
   558	        second_analysis.summary = "Second pass summary."
   559	        second_analysis.review_flags = ["manual_review"]
   560	        second_analysis.extraction_confidence = 0.31
   561	
   562	        mock_analyze.side_effect = [first_analysis, second_analysis]
   563	
   564	        first = ingest_source(
   565	            config,
   566	            source_path=source,
   567	            subtype="expert_interview",
   568	            event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   569	            client="ClientA",
   570	            engagement="DD Q1 2026",
   571	        )
   572	        first_fm = _parse_frontmatter(first.output_path)
   573	        assert first_fm["review_status"] == "clean"
   574	        assert first_fm["review_flags"] == []
   575	        assert first_fm["extraction_confidence"] == 0.91
   576	        assert "First pass summary." in first.output_path.read_text()
   577	
   578	        second = ingest_source(
   579	            config,
   580	            source_path=source,
   581	            subtype="expert_interview",
   582	            event_date=date(2026, 3, 21),
   583	            client="ClientA",
   584	            engagement="DD Q1 2026",
   585	        )
   586	
   587	        assert second.version == 2
   588	        fm = _parse_frontmatter(second.output_path)
   589	        assert fm["review_status"] == "flagged"
   590	        assert fm["review_flags"] == ["manual_review"]
   591	        assert fm["extraction_confidence"] == 0.31
   592	
   593	        body = second.output_path.read_text()
   594	        assert "Second pass summary." in body
   595	        assert "First pass summary." not in body
   596	
   597	        registry = json.loads((library / "registry.json").read_text())
   598	        entry = registry["decks"][second.interaction_id]
   599	        assert entry["review_status"] == "flagged"
   600	        assert entry["review_flags"] == ["manual_review"]
   601	        assert entry["extraction_confidence"] == 0.31
   602

   708	    @patch("folio.ingest.analyze_interaction_text")
   709	    def test_ingest_ambiguity_requires_target(self, mock_analyze, tmp_path):
   710	        library = _make_library(tmp_path)
   711	        config = FolioConfig(library_root=library)
   712	        mock_analyze.return_value = _analysis_result()
   713	
   714	        source_a = tmp_path / "transcripts" / "one.txt"
   715	        source_b = tmp_path / "transcripts" / "two.txt"
   716	        source_c = tmp_path / "transcripts" / "three.txt"
   717	        source_a.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   718	        for path in (source_a, source_b, source_c):
   719	            path.write_text("Shared transcript body.")
   720	
   721	        from folio.tracking.sources import compute_file_hash
   722	
   723	        shared_hash = compute_file_hash(source_a)
   724	        note_a = library / "ClientA" / "interactions" / "one" / "one.md"
   725	        note_b = library / "ClientA" / "interactions" / "two" / "two.md"
   726	        for note_path, source_rel, note_id in [
   727	            (note_a, "../../../transcripts/one.txt", "clienta_ddq126_meeting_20260321_alpha"),
   728	            (note_b, "../../../transcripts/two.txt", "clienta_ddq126_meeting_20260321_beta"),
   729	        ]:
   730	            note_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   731	            note_path.write_text(
   732	                "---\n"
   733	                f"id: {note_id}\n"
   734	                "title: Shared Meeting\n"
   735	                "type: interaction\n"
   736	                "subtype: client_meeting\n"
   737	                "status: complete\n"
   738	                "authority: captured\n"
   739	                "curation_level: L0\n"
   740	                "review_status: clean\n"
   741	                "review_flags: []\n"
   742	                "extraction_confidence: 0.87\n"
   743	                f"source_transcript: {source_rel}\n"
   744	                f"source_hash: {shared_hash}\n"
   745	                "version: 1\n"
   746	                "created: 2026-03-21T00:00:00Z\n"
   747	                "modified: 2026-03-21T00:00:00Z\n"
   748	                "converted: 2026-03-21T00:00:00Z\n"
   749	                "date: 2026-03-21\n"
   750	                "impacts: []\n"
   751	                "---\n"
   752	                "# Shared Meeting\n"
   753	            )
   754	
   755	        registry_data = {
   756	            "_schema_version": 1,
   757	            "decks": {
   758	                "clienta_ddq126_meeting_20260321_alpha": {
   759	                    **_sample_interaction_registry_entry(
   760	                        id="clienta_ddq126_meeting_20260321_alpha",
   761	                        title="Shared Meeting",
   762	                        markdown_path="ClientA/interactions/one/one.md",
   763	                        deck_dir="ClientA/interactions/one",
   764	                        source_relative_path="../../../transcripts/one.txt",
   765	                        source_hash=shared_hash,
   766	                        subtype="client_meeting",
   767	                    ),
   768	                    "source_type": None,
   769	                },
   770	                "clienta_ddq126_meeting_20260321_beta": {
   771	                    **_sample_interaction_registry_entry(
   772	                        id="clienta_ddq126_meeting_20260321_beta",
   773	                        title="Shared Meeting",
   774	                        markdown_path="ClientA/interactions/two/two.md",
   775	                        deck_dir="ClientA/interactions/two",
   776	                        source_relative_path="../../../transcripts/two.txt",
   777	                        source_hash=shared_hash,
   778	                        subtype="client_meeting",
   779	                    ),
   780	                    "source_type": None,
   781	                },
   782	            },
   783	        }
   784	        save_registry(library / "registry.json", registry_data)
   785

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""Transcript-native text normalization for caption formats."""
     2	
     3	from __future__ import annotations
     4	
     5	import html
     6	import re
     7	
     8	TRANSCRIPT_FORMAT_EXTENSIONS = frozenset({".vtt", ".srt"})
     9	
    10	_TIMING_LINE_RE = re.compile(
    11	    r"^\s*"
    12	    r"(?P<start>(?:\d{2}:)?\d{2}:\d{2}[\.,]\d{3})"
    13	    r"\s+-->\s+"
    14	    r"(?P<end>(?:\d{2}:)?\d{2}:\d{2}[\.,]\d{3})"
    15	    r"(?:\s+.*)?$"
    16	)
    17	_VOICE_TAG_RE = re.compile(r"<v(?:\.[^>\s]+)?\s+([^>]+)>", re.IGNORECASE)
    18	_TAG_RE = re.compile(r"<[^>]+>")
    19	_SPEAKER_PREFIX_RE = re.compile(r"^(?:[A-Z][\w .'\-/]{0,60}|Speaker \d+):\s+\S")
    20	
    21	
    22	def normalize_transcript_text(text: str, extension: str) -> str:
    23	    """Normalize VTT/SRT caption text into transcript-like plain text."""
    24	
    25	    normalized = text.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n")
    26	    extension = extension.lower()
    27	    if extension == ".vtt":
    28	        return _normalize_blocks(normalized, skip_vtt_control_blocks=True)
    29	    if extension == ".srt":
    30	        return _normalize_blocks(normalized, skip_vtt_control_blocks=False)
    31	    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported transcript format: {extension}")
    32	
    33	
    34	def _normalize_blocks(text: str, *, skip_vtt_control_blocks: bool) -> str:
    35	    lines: list[str] = []
    36	    for block in _split_blocks(text):
    37	        if not block:
    38	            continue
    39	
    40	        timing_index = _find_timing_line(block)
    41	        control_kind = _vtt_control_kind(block) if skip_vtt_control_blocks else ""
    42	        if control_kind in {"NOTE", "STYLE", "REGION"}:
    43	            continue
    44	        if control_kind == "WEBVTT" and timing_index is None:
    45	            continue
    46	        if timing_index is None:
    47	            continue
    48	
    49	        timing = _TIMING_LINE_RE.match(block[timing_index])
    50	        if timing is None:
    51	            continue
    52	
    53	        start = _normalize_timestamp(timing.group("start"))
    54	        end = _normalize_timestamp(timing.group("end"))
    55	        for utterance in _cue_utterances(block[timing_index + 1:]):
    56	            lines.append(f"[{start} - {end}] {utterance}")
    57	
    58	    return "\n".join(lines)
    59	
    60	
    61	def _split_blocks(text: str) -> list[list[str]]:
    62	    blocks: list[list[str]] = []
    63	    current: list[str] = []
    64	    for line in text.splitlines():
    65	        if line.strip():
    66	            current.append(line.strip("\ufeff"))
    67	            continue
    68	        if current:
    69	            blocks.append(current)
    70	            current = []
    71	    if current:
    72	        blocks.append(current)
    73	    return blocks
    74	
    75	
    76	def _vtt_control_kind(block: list[str]) -> str:
    77	    first = block[0].lstrip("\ufeff").strip()
    78	    upper = first.upper()
    79	    if upper.startswith("WEBVTT"):
    80	        return "WEBVTT"
    81	    if upper.startswith("NOTE"):
    82	        return "NOTE"
    83	    if upper in {"STYLE", "REGION"}:
    84	        return upper
    85	    return ""
    86	
    87	
    88	def _find_timing_line(block: list[str]) -> int | None:
    89	    for index, line in enumerate(block):
    90	        if _TIMING_LINE_RE.match(line):
    91	            return index
    92	    return None
    93	
    94	
    95	def _normalize_timestamp(value: str) -> str:
    96	    value = value.replace(",", ".")
    97	    parts = value.split(":")
    98	    if len(parts) == 2:
    99	        hours = "00"
   100	        minutes, seconds = parts
   101	    else:
   102	        hours, minutes, seconds = parts
   103	    return f"{int(hours):02d}:{int(minutes):02d}:{seconds}"
   104	
   105	
   106	def _cue_utterances(text_lines: list[str]) -> list[str]:
   107	    cleaned_lines = [
   108	        cleaned
   109	        for cleaned in (_clean_caption_text(line) for line in text_lines)
   110	        if cleaned
   111	    ]
   112	    if not cleaned_lines:
   113	        return []
   114	
   115	    utterances: list[str] = []
   116	    current: list[str] = []
   117	    for line in cleaned_lines:
   118	        if current and _SPEAKER_PREFIX_RE.match(line):
   119	            utterances.append(" ".join(current))
   120	            current = [line]
   121	        else:
   122	            current.append(line)
   123	    if current:
   124	        utterances.append(" ".join(current))
   125	    return utterances
   126	
   127	
   128	def _clean_caption_text(line: str) -> str:
   129	    voice_match = _VOICE_TAG_RE.search(line)
   130	    speaker = _clean_speaker(voice_match.group(1)) if voice_match else ""
   131	    cleaned = _VOICE_TAG_RE.sub("", line)
   132	    cleaned = _TAG_RE.sub("", cleaned)
   133	    cleaned = html.unescape(cleaned)
   134	    cleaned = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", cleaned).strip()
   135	    if speaker and cleaned:
   136	        return f"{speaker}: {cleaned}"
   137	    return cleaned
   138	
   139	
   140	def _clean_speaker(value: str) -> str:
   141	    cleaned = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", value).strip()
   142	    return cleaned.rstrip(":")

698:### Issue #69: Support transcript-native ingest formats like .vtt and .srt
716:That is too restrictive for the actual transcript artifacts people get from meeting tools. In practice, raw exports often come as:
718:- `.vtt` / `WEBVTT`
719:- `.srt`
720:- plain UTF-8 transcript files that may not have a `.txt` extension
722:In a real workflow today, I had a meeting transcript that Folio should absolutely be able to ingest directly, but instead I had to:
724:1. move the raw transcript out of the workspace root
727:4. run `folio ingest` on that surrogate file instead of the actual source transcript
729:That is a lot of avoidable friction for a transcript-ingestion command.
733:`folio ingest` rejects the raw transcript source based on extension.
741:And `.vtt` is likewise not supported even though it is a very common transcript format.
745:`folio ingest` should support transcript-native input formats directly, at minimum:
747:- `.vtt`
748:- `.srt`
754:- accept extensionless plaintext files when the content is clearly transcript-like / UTF-8 text
759:These formats are not edge cases. They are standard outputs from common meeting / transcription systems. If Folio is going to be the interaction-ingestion layer, it should ingest the raw artifacts users actually have, not force a manual conversion to markdown first.
763:For `.vtt` / `.srt` inputs:
765:- parse the transcript structure instead of rejecting by suffix
766:- strip / normalize transport markup (cue numbers, timestamps, `WEBVTT` header, etc.)
768:- feed the normalized transcript into the existing interaction-analysis path
774:- or require an explicit `--format plain` / `--format transcript` override
778:- `folio ingest meeting.vtt --type internal_sync ...` succeeds
779:- `folio ingest meeting.srt --type internal_sync ...` succeeds
780:- extracted interaction notes still preserve grounded findings, quotes, participants, and raw transcript sections
782:- docs/help text for `folio ingest` mention the supported transcript formats explicitly
786:The current docs describe interaction ingestion as taking a transcript/note file, which is exactly why the current extension restriction is surprising. Supporting raw transcript formats would make the CLI match the real user workflow much better.
832:I just ingested an `expert_interview` transcript that closed with three distinct forward-looking commitments:
958:- [ ] `folio ingest <client-meeting transcript>` produces a populated `### Next Steps` subsection when the transcript contains forward-looking commitments.
959:- [ ] `folio ingest <workshop transcript>` produces a populated `### Action Items` subsection.
962:- [ ] Re-ingesting an existing transcript with the new schema fills the new section without breaking existing fields.
993:Every transcript Folio ingests already contains the raw signal needed to answer *who talked, how much, and for how long* — speaker labels and second-resolution timestamps on every turn. Today we throw that signal away during ingest. The analysis pipeline only feeds the text into the LLM and never computes the deterministic per-speaker stats that fall out of the structure for free.
1003:Today I ingested an `expert_interview` (Altitude workspace, `library/altitude/spinoff/interactions/2026-04-24_20260424_jed_cairo_*`) — a ~24-minute Jed Cairo / Jonathan Oh conversation. Every turn in the source transcript looks like:
1020:- raw transcript callout
1033:- `folio/pipeline/interaction_analysis.py` parses the transcript only as text input to the LLM.
1037:- `registry.json` entries carry no speaker-balance data, so corpus queries like *"interactions where I spoke <30%"* are impossible without re-parsing every raw transcript.
1145:   - `parse_turns(source_text: str) -> list[Turn]` — regex over the standard `HH:MM:SS Speaker Name` line pattern; supports the existing transcript convention (one timestamp + speaker per turn block).
1181:6. **Speaker-name normalization** — defer to existing entity resolution where possible; canonical name takes precedence over transcript label, but `aliases` are accepted as same-speaker (so "Jonathan" and "Jonathan Oh" don't show up as two speakers).
1183:7. **Graceful degradation** — if the transcript has no parseable timestamps/speakers (e.g. a free-form interview note), skip the pass silently and emit `review_flag: speaker_analytics_unavailable`.
1187:- Empty / malformed transcripts → no `## Speaker Analytics` section emitted; new flag in `review_flags` (`speaker_analytics_unavailable`) so it's discoverable.
1194:- [ ] `folio ingest <transcript with timestamps + speaker labels>` produces a populated `## Speaker Analytics` section + `speakers:` frontmatter block.
1199:- [ ] Re-ingesting an existing transcript with `--no-cache` populates the new fields without breaking existing fields.

docs/validation/strict_p3_rerun_2026_05_12/review-board/folio-github-closeout-v1-0-0-D.2-claude-sonnet-peer.md:31:- **`folio/pipeline/transcript_formats.py`** — present and fully implemented. Exports `normalize_transcript_text(text, extension)` supporting `.vtt` and `.srt`. The module correctly strips WEBVTT headers, NOTE/STYLE/REGION control blocks, cue sequence numbers, `-->` timing lines, inline HTML tags (`<v>`, `<b>`, etc.), and normalises timestamps to `HH:MM:SS.mmm` form. Multi-speaker voice tags (`<v Speaker Name>`) are resolved to `Speaker Name: utterance` per cue. Wrapped lines within a single cue are joined before speaker-boundary splitting.
